Index[](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/indices.html#index)
------------------------------------------------------------------

The following sections only cover conforming elements and features.

### Elements[](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/indices.html#elements-3)

*This section is non-normative.*

| `[video](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/media.html#the-video-element)` | Video player | [flow](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#flow-content-2); [phrasing](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#phrasing-content-2); [embedded](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#embedded-content-category); [interactive](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#interactive-content-2); [palpable](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#palpable-content-2) | [phrasing](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#phrasing-content-2) | `[source](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/embedded-content.html#the-source-element)`*; `[track](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/media.html#the-track-element)`*; [transparent](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#transparent)* | [globals](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#global-attributes); `[src](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/media.html#attr-media-src)`; `[crossorigin](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/media.html#attr-media-crossorigin)`; `[poster](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/media.html#attr-video-poster)`; `[preload](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/media.html#attr-media-preload)`; `[autoplay](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/media.html#attr-media-autoplay)`; `[playsinline](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/media.html#attr-video-playsinline)`; `[loop](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/media.html#attr-media-loop)`; `[muted](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/media.html#attr-media-muted)`; `[controls](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/media.html#attr-media-controls)`; `[width](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/embedded-content-other.html#attr-dim-width)`; `[height](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/embedded-content-other.html#attr-dim-height)` | `[HTMLVideoElement](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/media.html#htmlvideoelement)` |
| `[wbr](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/text-level-semantics.html#the-wbr-element)` | Line breaking opportunity | [flow](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#flow-content-2); [phrasing](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#phrasing-content-2) | [phrasing](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#phrasing-content-2) | empty | [globals](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#global-attributes) | `[HTMLElement](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#htmlelement)` |
| [autonomous custom elements](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/custom-elements.html#autonomous-custom-element) | Author-defined elements | [flow](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#flow-content-2); [phrasing](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#phrasing-content-2); [palpable](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#palpable-content-2) | [flow](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#flow-content-2); [phrasing](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#phrasing-content-2) | [transparent](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#transparent) | [globals](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#global-attributes); any, as decided by the element's author | Supplied by the element's author (inherits from `[HTMLElement](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#htmlelement)`) |

An asterisk (*) in a cell indicates that the actual rules are more complicated than indicated in the table above.

† Categories in the "Parents" column refer to parents that list the given categories in their content model, not to elements that themselves are in those categories. For example, the `[a](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/text-level-semantics.html#the-a-element)` element's "Parents" column says "phrasing", so any element whose content model contains the "phrasing" category could be a parent of an `[a](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/text-level-semantics.html#the-a-element)` element. Since the "flow" category includes all the "phrasing" elements, that means the `[th](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/tables.html#the-th-element)` element could be a parent to an `[a](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/text-level-semantics.html#the-a-element)` element.

*This section is non-normative.*

a `[map](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/image-maps.html#the-map-element)` element); `[link](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/semantics.html#the-link-element)` (if it is [allowed in the body](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/semantics.html#allowed-in-the-body)); `[main](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/grouping-content.html#the-main-element)` (if it is a [hierarchically correct `main` element](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/grouping-content.html#hierarchically-correct-main-element)); `[meta](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/semantics.html#the-meta-element)` (if the `[itemprop](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/microdata.html#names:-the-itemprop-attribute)` attribute is present) |
| [Sectioning content](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#sectioning-content-2) | `[article](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/sections.html#the-article-element)`; `[aside](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/sections.html#the-aside-element)`; `[nav](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/sections.html#the-nav-element)`; `[section](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/sections.html#the-section-element)` | --- |
| [Heading content](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#heading-content-2) | `[h1](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/sections.html#the-h1,-h2,-h3,-h4,-h5,-and-h6-elements)`; `[h2](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/sections.html#the-h1,-h2,-h3,-h4,-h5,-and-h6-elements)`; `[h3](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/sections.html#the-h1,-h2,-h3,-h4,-h5,-and-h6-elements)`; `[h4](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/sections.html#the-h1,-h2,-h3,-h4,-h5,-and-h6-elements)`; `[h5](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/sections.html#the-h1,-h2,-h3,-h4,-h5,-and-h6-elements)`; `[h6](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/sections.html#the-h1,-h2,-h3,-h4,-h5,-and-h6-elements)`; `[hgroup](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/sections.html#the-hgroup-element)` | --- |

children include at least one `[li](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/grouping-content.html#the-li-element)` element); `[ul](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/grouping-content.html#the-ul-element)` (if the element's children include at least one `[li](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/grouping-content.html#the-li-element)` element); [Text](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#text-content) that is not [inter-element whitespace](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#inter-element-whitespace) |
| [Script-supporting elements](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#script-supporting-elements-2) | `[script](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/scripting.html#the-script-element)`; `[template](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/scripting.html#the-template-element)` | --- |

### Attributes[](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/indices.html#attributes-3)

*This section is non-normative.*

List of attributes (excluding event handler content attributes)
| Attribute | Element(s) | Description | Value |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `abbr` | `[th](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/tables.html#attr-th-abbr)` | Alternative label to use for the header cell when referencing the cell in other contexts | [Text](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#attribute-text)* |
| `accept` | `[input](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/input.html#attr-input-accept)` | Hint for expected file type in [file upload controls](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/input.html#file-upload-state-(type=file)) | [Set of comma-separated tokens](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/common-microsyntaxes.html#set-of-comma-separated-tokens)* consisting of [valid MIME type strings with no parameters](https://mimesniff.spec.whatwg.org/#valid-mime-type-with-no-parameters) or `audio/*`, `video/*`, or `image/*` |
| `accept-charset` | `[form](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/forms.html#attr-form-accept-charset)` | Character encodings to use for [form submission](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/form-control-infrastructure.html#form-submission-2) | [ASCII case-insensitive](https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#ascii-case-insensitive) match for "`UTF-8`" |
| `accesskey` | [HTML elements](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interaction.html#the-accesskey-attribute) | Keyboard shortcut to activate or focus element | [Ordered set of unique space-separated tokens](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/common-microsyntaxes.html#ordered-set-of-unique-space-separated-tokens), none of which are [identical to](https://infra.spec.whatwg.org/#string-is) another, each consisting of one code point in length |
| `action` | `[form](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/form-control-infrastructure.html#attr-fs-action)` | [URL](https://url.spec.whatwg.org/#concept-url) to use for [form submission](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/form-control-infrastructure.html#form-submission-2) | [Valid non-empty URL potentially surrounded by spaces](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/urls-and-fetching.html#valid-non-empty-url-potentially-surrounded-by-spaces) |
| `allow` | `[iframe](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/iframe-embed-object.html#attr-iframe-allow)` | [Permissions policy](https://w3c.github.io/webappsec-feature-policy/#permissions-policy) to be applied to the `[iframe](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/iframe-embed-object.html#the-iframe-element)`'s contents | [Serialized permissions policy](https://w3c.github.io/webappsec-feature-policy/#serialized-permissions-policy) |
| `allowfullscreen` | `[iframe](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/iframe-embed-object.html#attr-iframe-allowfullscreen)` | Whether to allow the `[iframe](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/iframe-embed-object.html#the-iframe-element)`'s contents to use `[requestFullscreen()](https://fullscreen.spec.whatwg.org/#dom-element-requestfullscreen)` | [Boolean attribute](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/common-microsyntaxes.html#boolean-attribute) |
| `alt` | `[area](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/image-maps.html#attr-area-alt)`; `[img](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/embedded-content.html#attr-img-alt)`; `[input](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/input.html#attr-input-alt)` | Replacement text for use when images are not available | [Text](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#attribute-text)* |
| `as` | `[link](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/semantics.html#attr-link-as)` | [Potential destination](https://fetch.spec.whatwg.org/#concept-potential-destination) for a preload request (for `[rel](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/semantics.html#attr-link-rel)`="`[preload](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/links.html#link-type-preload)`" and `[rel](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/semantics.html#attr-link-rel)`="`[modulepreload](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/links.html#link-type-modulepreload)`") | [Potential destination](https://fetch.spec.whatwg.org/#concept-potential-destination), for `[rel](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/semantics.html#attr-link-rel)`="`[preload](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/links.html#link-type-preload)`"; [script-like destination](https://fetch.spec.whatwg.org/#request-destination-script-like), for `[rel](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/semantics.html#attr-link-rel)`="`[modulepreload](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/links.html#link-type-modulepreload)`" |
| `async` | `[script](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/scripting.html#attr-script-async)` | Execute script when available, without blocking while fetching | [Boolean attribute](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/common-microsyntaxes.html#boolean-attribute) |
| `autocapitalize` | [HTML elements](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interaction.html#attr-autocapitalize) | Recommended autocapitalization behavior (for supported input methods) | "`[on](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interaction.html#attr-autocapitalize-on)`"; "`[off](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interaction.html#attr-autocapitalize-off)`"; "`[none](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interaction.html#attr-autocapitalize-none)`"; "`[sentences](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interaction.html#attr-autocapitalize-sentences)`"; "`[words](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interaction.html#attr-autocapitalize-words)`"; "`[characters](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interaction.html#attr-autocapitalize-characters)`" |
| `autocomplete` | `[form](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/forms.html#attr-form-autocomplete)` | Default setting for autofill feature for controls in the form | "`on`"; "`off`" |
| `autocomplete` | `[input](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/form-control-infrastructure.html#attr-fe-autocomplete)`; `[select](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/form-control-infrastructure.html#attr-fe-autocomplete)`; `[textarea](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/form-control-infrastructure.html#attr-fe-autocomplete)` | Hint for form autofill feature | [Autofill field](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/form-control-infrastructure.html#autofill-field) name and related tokens* |
| `autofocus` | [HTML elements](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interaction.html#attr-fe-autofocus) | Automatically focus the element when the page is loaded | [Boolean attribute](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/common-microsyntaxes.html#boolean-attribute) |
| `autoplay` | `[audio](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/media.html#attr-media-autoplay)`; `[video](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/media.html#attr-media-autoplay)` | Hint that the [media resource](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/media.html#media-resource) can be started automatically when the page is loaded | [Boolean attribute](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/common-microsyntaxes.html#boolean-attribute) |

**✔**MDN

List of event handler content attributes
| Attribute | Element(s) | Description | Value |

### Events[](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/indices.html#events-2)

*This section is non-normative.*

List of events
| Event | Interface | Interesting targets | Description |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `DOMContentLoaded`

**✔**MDN

 | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | `[Document](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#document)` | Fired at the `[Document](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#document)` once the parser has finished |
| `afterprint`

**✔**MDN

 | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` | Fired at the `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` after printing |
| `beforeprint`

**✔**MDN

 | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` | Fired at the `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` before printing |
| `beforeunload`

**✔**MDN

 | `[BeforeUnloadEvent](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/browsing-the-web.html#beforeunloadevent)` | `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` | Fired at the `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` when the page is about to be unloaded, in case the page would like to show a warning prompt |
| `blur` | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)`, elements | Fired at nodes when they stop being [focused](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interaction.html#focused) |
| `cancel`

MDN

 | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | `[dialog](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interactive-elements.html#the-dialog-element)` elements, `[input](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/input.html#the-input-element)` elements | Fired at `[dialog](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interactive-elements.html#the-dialog-element)` elements when they are canceled by the user (e.g., by pressing the Escape key), or at `[input](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/input.html#the-input-element)` elements in the [File](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/input.html#file-upload-state-(type=file)) state when the user does not change their selection |
| `change` | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | Form controls | Fired at controls when the user commits a value change (see also the `[input](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/indices.html#event-input)` event) |
| `[click](https://w3c.github.io/uievents/#event-type-click)` | `[PointerEvent](https://w3c.github.io/pointerevents/#pointerevent-interface)` | Elements | Normally a mouse event; also synthetically fired at an element before its [activation behavior](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#eventtarget-activation-behavior) is run, when an element is activated from a non-pointer input device (e.g. a keyboard) |
| `close`

**⚠**MDN

 | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` or `[CloseEvent](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/web-sockets.html#closeevent)` | `[dialog](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interactive-elements.html#the-dialog-element)` elements, `[WebSocket](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/web-sockets.html#websocket)` | Fired at `[dialog](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interactive-elements.html#the-dialog-element)` elements when they are closed, and at `[WebSocket](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/web-sockets.html#websocket)` objects when the connection is terminated |
| `connect`

MDN

 | `[MessageEvent](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/comms.html#messageevent)` | `[SharedWorkerGlobalScope](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/workers.html#sharedworkerglobalscope)` | Fired at a shared worker's global scope when a new client connects |
| `contextlost` | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | `[canvas](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/canvas.html#the-canvas-element)` elements, `[OffscreenCanvas](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/canvas.html#offscreencanvas)` objects | Fired when the corresponding `[CanvasRenderingContext2D](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/canvas.html#canvasrenderingcontext2d)` or `[OffscreenCanvasRenderingContext2D](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/canvas.html#offscreencanvasrenderingcontext2d)` is lost |
| `contextmenu`

**✔**MDN

 | `[PointerEvent](https://w3c.github.io/pointerevents/#pointerevent-interface)` | Elements | Fired at elements when the user requests their context menu |
| `contextrestored` | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | `[canvas](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/canvas.html#the-canvas-element)` elements, `[OffscreenCanvas](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/canvas.html#offscreencanvas)` objects | Fired when the corresponding `[CanvasRenderingContext2D](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/canvas.html#canvasrenderingcontext2d)` or `[OffscreenCanvasRenderingContext2D](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/canvas.html#offscreencanvasrenderingcontext2d)` is restored after being lost |
| `copy` | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | Elements | Fired at elements when the user copies data to the clipboard |
| `cut` | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | Elements | Fired at elements when the user copies the selected data on the clipboard and removes the selection from the document |
| `error`

**✔**MDN

 | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` or `[ErrorEvent](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/webappapis.html#errorevent)` | Global scope objects, `[Worker](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/workers.html#worker)` objects, elements, networking-related objects | Fired when unexpected errors occur (e.g. networking errors, script errors, decoding errors) |
| `focus` | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)`, elements | Fired at nodes [gaining focus](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interaction.html#gains-focus) |
| `formdata`

**✔**MDN

 | `[FormDataEvent](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/form-control-infrastructure.html#formdataevent)` | `[form](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/forms.html#the-form-element)` elements | Fired at a `[form](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/forms.html#the-form-element)` element when it is [constructing the entry list](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/form-control-infrastructure.html#constructing-the-form-data-set) |
| `hashchange`

**✔**MDN

 | `[HashChangeEvent](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/browsing-the-web.html#hashchangeevent)` | `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` | Fired at the `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` when the [fragment](https://url.spec.whatwg.org/#concept-url-fragment) part of the document's [URL](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#concept-document-url) changes |
| `input`

**✔**MDN

 | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | Form controls | Fired at controls when the user changes the value (see also the `[change](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/indices.html#event-change)` event) |
| `invalid`

**✔**MDN

 | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | Form controls | Fired at controls during form validation if they do not satisfy their constraints |
| `languagechange`

**✔**MDN

 | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | Global scope objects | Fired at the global scope object when the user's preferred languages change |
| `load` | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)`, elements | Fired at the `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` when the document has finished loading; fired at an element containing a resource (e.g. `[img](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/embedded-content.html#the-img-element)`, `[embed](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/iframe-embed-object.html#the-embed-element)`) when its resource has finished loading |
| `message`

**✔**MDN

 | `[MessageEvent](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/comms.html#messageevent)` | `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)`, `[EventSource](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/server-sent-events.html#eventsource)`, `[WebSocket](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/web-sockets.html#websocket)`, `[MessagePort](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/web-messaging.html#messageport)`, `[BroadcastChannel](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/web-messaging.html#broadcastchannel)`, `[DedicatedWorkerGlobalScope](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/workers.html#dedicatedworkerglobalscope)`, `[Worker](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/workers.html#worker)`, `[ServiceWorkerContainer](https://w3c.github.io/ServiceWorker/#serviceworkercontainer)` | Fired at an object when it receives a message |
| `messageerror`

**✔**MDN

 | `[MessageEvent](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/comms.html#messageevent)` | `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)`, `[MessagePort](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/web-messaging.html#messageport)`, `[BroadcastChannel](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/web-messaging.html#broadcastchannel)`, `[DedicatedWorkerGlobalScope](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/workers.html#dedicatedworkerglobalscope)`, `[Worker](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/workers.html#worker)`, `[ServiceWorkerContainer](https://w3c.github.io/ServiceWorker/#serviceworkercontainer)` | Fired at an object when it receives a message that cannot be deserialized |
| `offline`

**✔**MDN

 | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | Global scope objects | Fired at the global scope object when the network connections fails |
| `online`

**✔**MDN

 | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | Global scope objects | Fired at the global scope object when the network connections returns |
| `open`

**✔**MDN

 | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | `[EventSource](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/server-sent-events.html#eventsource)`, `[WebSocket](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/web-sockets.html#websocket)` | Fired at networking-related objects when a connection is established |
| `pagehide`

**✔**MDN

 | `[PageTransitionEvent](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/browsing-the-web.html#pagetransitionevent)` | `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` | Fired at the `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` when the page's entry in the [session history](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/history.html#session-history) stops being the [current entry](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/history.html#current-entry) |
| `pageshow`

**✔**MDN

 | `[PageTransitionEvent](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/browsing-the-web.html#pagetransitionevent)` | `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` | Fired at the `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` when the page's entry in the [session history](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/history.html#session-history) becomes the [current entry](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/history.html#current-entry) |
| `paste` | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | Elements | Fired at elements when the user will insert the clipboard data in the most suitable format (if any) supported for the given context |
| `popstate`

**✔**MDN

 | `[PopStateEvent](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/browsing-the-web.html#popstateevent)` | `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` | Fired at the `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` when the user navigates the [session history](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/history.html#session-history) |
| `readystatechange`

**✔**MDN

 | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | `[Document](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#document)` | Fired at the `[Document](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#document)` when it finishes parsing and again when all its subresources have finished loading |
| `rejectionhandled` | `[PromiseRejectionEvent](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/webappapis.html#promiserejectionevent)` | Global scope objects | Fired at global scope objects when a previously-unhandled promise rejection becomes handled |
| `reset`

**✔**MDN

 | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | `[form](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/forms.html#the-form-element)` elements | Fired at a `[form](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/forms.html#the-form-element)` element when it is [reset](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/form-control-infrastructure.html#concept-form-reset) |
| `securitypolicyviolation` | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | Elements | Fired at elements when a Content Security Policy violation is generated [[CSP]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsCSP) |
| `select` | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | Form controls | Fired at form controls when their text selection is adjusted (whether by an API or by the user) |
| `slotchange`

**✔**MDN

 | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | `[slot](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/scripting.html#the-slot-element)` elements | Fired at `[slot](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/scripting.html#the-slot-element)` elements when their [assigned nodes](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#slot-assigned-nodes) change |
| `storage`

**✔**MDN

 | `[StorageEvent](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/webstorage.html#storageevent)` | `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` | Fired at `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` event when the corresponding `[localStorage](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/webstorage.html#dom-localstorage)` or `[sessionStorage](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/webstorage.html#dom-sessionstorage)` storage areas change |
| `submit`

**✔**MDN

 | `[SubmitEvent](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/form-control-infrastructure.html#submitevent)` | `[form](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/forms.html#the-form-element)` elements | Fired at a `[form](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/forms.html#the-form-element)` element when it is [submitted](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/form-control-infrastructure.html#concept-form-submit) |
| `toggle`

**✔**MDN

 | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | `[details](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interactive-elements.html#the-details-element)` element | Fired at `[details](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/interactive-elements.html#the-details-element)` elements when they open or close |
| `unhandledrejection`

**✔**MDN

 | `[PromiseRejectionEvent](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/webappapis.html#promiserejectionevent)` | Global scope objects | Fired at global scope objects when a promise rejection goes unhandled |
| `unload`

**✔**MDN

 | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` | Fired at the `[Window](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/window-object.html#window)` object when the page is going away |
| `visibilitychange` | `[Event](https://dom.spec.whatwg.org/#interface-event)` | `[Document](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#document)` | Fired at the `[Document](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dom.html#document)` object when the page becomes visible or hidden to the user. [[PAGEVIS]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsPAGEVIS) |

See also [media element events](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/media.html#mediaevents) and [drag-and-drop events](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/dnd.html#dndevents).

### MIME Types[](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/indices.html#mime-types-2)

*This section is non-normative.*

The following MIME types are mentioned in this specification:

`application/atom+xml`

Atom [[ATOM]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsATOM)

`application/ecmascript`

JavaScript (legacy type) [[JAVASCRIPT]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJAVASCRIPT)

`application/javascript`

JavaScript (legacy type) [[JAVASCRIPT]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJAVASCRIPT)

`application/json`

JSON [[JSON]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJSON)

`application/x-ecmascript`

JavaScript (legacy type) [[JAVASCRIPT]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJAVASCRIPT)

`application/x-javascript`

JavaScript (legacy type) [[JAVASCRIPT]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJAVASCRIPT)

[`application/octet-stream`](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc2046#section-4.5.1)

Generic binary data [[RFC2046]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsRFC2046)

`[application/microdata+json](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/iana.html#application/microdata+json)`

Microdata as JSON

`application/rss+xml`

RSS

`[application/x-www-form-urlencoded](https://url.spec.whatwg.org/#concept-urlencoded)`

Form submission

`[application/xhtml+xml](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/iana.html#application/xhtml+xml)`

HTML

`application/xml`

XML [[XML]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsXML) [[RFC7303]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsRFC7303)

`image/gif`

GIF images [[GIF]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsGIF)

`image/jpeg`

JPEG images [[JPEG]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJPEG)

`image/png`

PNG images [[PNG]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsPNG)

`image/svg+xml`

SVG images [[SVG]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsSVG)

`multipart/form-data`

Form submission [[RFC7578]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsRFC7578)

`multipart/mixed`

Generic mixed content [[RFC2046]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsRFC2046)

`[multipart/x-mixed-replace](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/iana.html#multipart/x-mixed-replace)`

Streaming server push

`text/css`

CSS [[CSS]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsCSS)

`text/ecmascript`

JavaScript (legacy type) [[JAVASCRIPT]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJAVASCRIPT)

`[text/event-stream](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/iana.html#text/event-stream)`

Server-sent event streams

`text/javascript`

JavaScript [[JAVASCRIPT]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJAVASCRIPT)

`text/javascript1.0`

JavaScript (legacy type) [[JAVASCRIPT]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJAVASCRIPT)

`text/javascript1.1`

JavaScript (legacy type) [[JAVASCRIPT]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJAVASCRIPT)

`text/javascript1.2`

JavaScript (legacy type) [[JAVASCRIPT]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJAVASCRIPT)

`text/javascript1.3`

JavaScript (legacy type) [[JAVASCRIPT]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJAVASCRIPT)

`text/javascript1.4`

JavaScript (legacy type) [[JAVASCRIPT]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJAVASCRIPT)

`text/javascript1.5`

JavaScript (legacy type) [[JAVASCRIPT]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJAVASCRIPT)

`text/jscript`

JavaScript (legacy type) [[JAVASCRIPT]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJAVASCRIPT)

`text/json`

JSON (legacy type)

`text/livescript`

JavaScript (legacy type) [[JAVASCRIPT]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJAVASCRIPT)

[`text/plain`](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc2046#section-4.1.3)

Generic plain text [[RFC2046]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsRFC2046) [[RFC3676]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsRFC3676)

`[text/html](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/iana.html#text/html)`

HTML

`[text/ping](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/iana.html#text/ping)`

Hyperlink auditing

`text/uri-list`

List of URLs [[RFC2483]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsRFC2483)

`text/vcard`

vCard [[RFC6350]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsRFC6350)

`text/vtt`

WebVTT [[WEBVTT]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsWEBVTT)

`text/x-ecmascript`

JavaScript (legacy type) [[JAVASCRIPT]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJAVASCRIPT)

`text/x-javascript`

JavaScript (legacy type) [[JAVASCRIPT]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsJAVASCRIPT)

`text/xml`

XML [[XML]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsXML) [[RFC7303]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsRFC7303)

[`video/mp4`](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc4337#section-3)

MPEG-4 video [[RFC4337]](https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/references.html#refsRFC4337)

`video/mpeg`
